graph TD
    CRB[ClusterRoleBinding: karpenter-core]
    CR[ClusterRole: karpenter-core]
    SA[ServiceAccount: karpenter]
    
    CRB -->|roleRef| CR
    CRB -->|subjects| SA
    
    CR -->|Read Permissions| ReadResources[Read Resources]
    CR -->|Write Permissions| WriteResources[Write Resources]
    
    ReadResources -->|karpenter.sh| R1[nodepools, nodeclaims]
    ReadResources -->|core| R2[pods, nodes, PVs, PVCs, namespaces]
    ReadResources -->|storage.k8s.io| R3[storageclasses, csinodes]
    ReadResources -->|apps| R4[daemonsets, deployments, replicasets, statefulsets]
    ReadResources -->|policy| R5[poddisruptionbudgets]
    ReadResources -->|admissionregistration| R6[webhook configs]
    
    WriteResources -->|karpenter.sh| W1[create/delete/update nodeclaims]
    WriteResources -->|karpenter.sh| W2[update/patch nodepools]
    WriteResources -->|core| W3[create/patch events]
    WriteResources -->|core| W4[patch/delete nodes]
    WriteResources -->|core| W5[create pod evictions]
    WriteResources -->|admissionregistration| W6[update webhook configs]

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    Start[Karpenter ServiceAccount] --> Binding[ClusterRoleBinding]
    Binding --> Role[ClusterRole]
    
    Role --> ReadOps[Read Operations]
    Role --> WriteOps[Write Operations]
    
    ReadOps --> ReadVerbs[get, list, watch]
    WriteOps --> WriteVerbs[create, delete, update, patch]
    
    ReadVerbs --> KarpenterRead[Karpenter Resources]
    ReadVerbs --> K8sRead[Core K8s Resources]
    ReadVerbs --> StorageRead[Storage Resources]
    ReadVerbs --> AppsRead[Apps Resources]
    
    WriteVerbs --> KarpenterWrite[Karpenter Resources]
    WriteVerbs --> K8sWrite[Core K8s Resources]
    WriteVerbs --> WebhookWrite[Webhook Configs]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class ClusterRoleBinding {
        +metadata
        +roleRef
        +subjects[]
    }
    
    class ClusterRole {
        +metadata
        +rules[]
    }
    
    class ServiceAccount {
        +name
        +namespace
    }
    
    class Rule {
        +apiGroups[]
        +resources[]
        +verbs[]
        +resourceNames[]
    }
    
    ClusterRoleBinding --> ClusterRole : references
    ClusterRoleBinding --> ServiceAccount : binds to
    ClusterRole --> Rule : contains
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> ServiceAccountCreated
    ServiceAccountCreated --> ClusterRoleCreated : Define permissions
    ClusterRoleCreated --> ClusterRoleBindingCreated : Bind role
    ClusterRoleBindingCreated --> ReadPermissions : Grant read access
    ClusterRoleBindingCreated --> WritePermissions : Grant write access
    
    ReadPermissions --> MonitorResources : Watch karpenter.sh resources
    ReadPermissions --> MonitorK8s : Watch core K8s resources
    ReadPermissions --> MonitorStorage : Watch storage resources
    
    WritePermissions --> ManageNodeClaims : Create/delete nodeclaims
    WritePermissions --> ManageNodePools : Update nodepools
    WritePermissions --> ManageNodes : Patch/delete nodes
    WritePermissions --> CreateEvents : Create events
    WritePermissions --> EvictPods : Create pod evictions
    
    MonitorResources --> [*]
    MonitorK8s --> [*]
    MonitorStorage --> [*]
    ManageNodeClaims --> [*]
    ManageNodePools --> [*]
    ManageNodes --> [*]
    CreateEvents --> [*]
    EvictPods --> [*]
```
